Slow leak in Driver-side Rear tire. Likely due to the rim, though could be something else.
Normal wear and tear for a vehicle this age.
Missing CD changer.
Cruise Control not functioning.
Needs new accessory belt.

The Ugly:
There is an electrical issue in either a sensor or wiring harness that is causing a slow drain on the battery and throwing a vague engine code. When driven regularly, the drain isn't an issue, but when sitting for months on end, it will kill the battery.
Above mentioned sensor/harness issue causes intermittent issues with engine.

Why are we selling it? Don't need it. It was the spare car for a long time and now it's taking up space in the driveway.
All issues can be resolved by someone willing to give it some TLC, but that isn't us.

Priced to move based on market and known problems.
